validation_script
function compare(one,op,two)

//VALIDATION SCRIPT
/*

Validates a question, using a user defined operator, against another question

EXAMPLE: compare('q1','!=','100') q1 must equal to 100

for more information: http://hab.pslresearch.com/wi/p9876082/ctl.asp

*/

{

/*set question variables and check if it is a question value or a number*/

var v1;    //used for evaluation stores 'f(q1)'
var v1i;  //stores only 'q1' value, sent to ErrBegTex
var v2;  //stores value of question user is evaluating against
var flg;//flag - if compound(multi) it gets flagged


/*sets flag if question is a compound, for special validation msg*/
var v= f(one);

if (v.COMPOUND){
flg = 1;
v1i = Sum(f(one));
}

else{
flg = 0;
v1i = one;
}
/*automatically evaluates 'one' as a question and sums it's value as it can never be a number*/

v1 = Sum(f(one)); 

/* test if validating against a number or a question */

if (isNaN(two)){
v2 = Sum(f(two));
}

else
v2 = two;


/*Verify what kind of comparison operation and then compare and display appropriate error message */
 
  
switch (op) {
 
case '>=':
 
if (v1>=v2){

RaiseError();
ClearErrorMessage();
SetQuestionErrorMessage(54,ErrBegTxt(flg,'af',v1i)+"moet gelyk minder wees as "+v2+". . Dankie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(9,ErrBegTxt(flg,'en',v1i)+"must be less than "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(12,ErrBegTxt(flg,'fr',v1i)+"devrait être inférieure à "+v2+". Merci!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(7,ErrBegTxt(flg,'de',v1i)+"sollte kleiner als "+v2+" sein. Danke!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(16,ErrBegTxt(flg,'it',v1i)+"deve essere inferiore a "+v2+". Grazie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(10,ErrBegTxt(flg,'es',v1i)+"debe ser inferior a "+v2+". Muchas gracias!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(22,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"deverá ser abaixo a "+v2+". Obrigado/a!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(20,ErrBegTxt(flg,'no',v1i)+"må være mindre enn "+v2+". Takk!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(6,ErrBegTxt(flg,'da',v1i)+"skal være mindre end "+v2+". Mange tak!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(29,ErrBegTxt(flg,'sv',v1i)+"måste vara mindre än "+v2+". Tack!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(31,ErrBegTxt(flg,'tr',v1i)+"en fazla "+v2+" olmalidir. Tesekkür ederiz!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(18,ErrBegTxt(flg,'ko',v1i)+v2+" &#48372;&#45796; &#52964;&#50556; &#54633;&#45768;&#45796;.  &#44048;&#49324;&#54633;&#45768;&#45796;!");

}
break;
 
case '<=':
 
if (v1<=v2){

RaiseError();

SetQuestionErrorMessage(9,ErrBegTxt(flg,'en',v1i)+"must be greater than "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(54,ErrBegTxt(flg,'af',v1i)+"moet gelyk wees aan of meer as "+v2+". Dankie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(12,ErrBegTxt(flg,'fr',v1i)+"devrait être supérieure à "+v2+". Merci!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(7,ErrBegTxt(flg,'de',v1i)+"sollte grösser als "+v2+" sein. Danke!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(16,ErrBegTxt(flg,'it',v1i)+"deve essere maggiore a "+v2+". Grazie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(10,ErrBegTxt(flg,'es',v1i)+"debe ser superior a "+v2+". Muchas gracias!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(22,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"Sua resposta deverá ser maior do que "+v2+". Obrigado/a!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(20,ErrBegTxt(flg,'no',v1i)+"må være større enn "+v2+". Takk!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(6,ErrBegTxt(flg,'da',v1i)+"skal være større end "+v2+". Mange tak!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(29,ErrBegTxt(flg,'sv',v1i)+"måste vara större än "+v2+". Tack!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(31,ErrBegTxt(flg,'tr',v1i)+"en az "+v2+" olmalidir. Tesekkür ederiz!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(18,ErrBegTxt(flg,'ko',v1i)+v2+" &#48372;&#45796; &#52964;&#50556; &#54633;&#45768;&#45796;.  &#44048;&#49324;&#54633;&#45768;&#45796;!");

}
break;
 
case '>':
 
if (v1>v2){
RaiseError();
SetQuestionErrorMessage(9,ErrBegTxt(flg,'en',v1i)+"must be less than or equal to "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(54,ErrBegTxt(flg,'af',v1i)+"moet gelyk wees aan of minder wees as "+v2+". Dankie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(12,ErrBegTxt(flg,'fr',v1i)+"devrait être inférieure ou égale à "+v2+". Merci!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(7,ErrBegTxt(flg,'de',v1i)+"sollte kleiner oder gleich "+v2+" sein. Danke!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(16,ErrBegTxt(flg,'it',v1i)+"deve essere inferiore o uguale a "+v2+". Grazie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(10,ErrBegTxt(flg,'es',v1i)+"debe ser inferior o igual a "+v2+". Muchas gracias!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(22,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"deverá ser abaixo ou igual a "+v2+". Obrigado/a!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(20,ErrBegTxt(flg,'no',v1i)+"må være mindre enn eller tilsvare "+v2+". Takk!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(6,ErrBegTxt(flg,'da',v1i)+"skal være mindre end eller lig med "+v2+". Mange tak!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(29,ErrBegTxt(flg,'sv',v1i)+"måste vara mindre än eller lika med "+v2+". Tack!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(31,ErrBegTxt(flg,'tr',v1i)+"en fazla veya tam olarak "+v2+" olmalidir. Tesekkür ederiz!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(18,ErrBegTxt(flg,'ko',v1i)+v2+" &#48372;&#45796; &#51089;&#44144;&#45208;  &#46041;&#46321;&#54644;&#50556; &#54633;&#45768;&#45796;. &#44048;&#49324;&#54633;&#45768;&#45796;!");

}
break;
 
case '<':
 
if (v1<v2){

RaiseError();

SetQuestionErrorMessage(9,ErrBegTxt(flg,'en',v1i)+"must be greater than or equal to "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(54,ErrBegTxt(flg,'af',v1i)+"moet gelyk wees aan of meer as "+v2+". Dankie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(12,ErrBegTxt(flg,'fr',v1i)+"doit être égale ou supérieure à "+v2+". Merci!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(7,ErrBegTxt(flg,'de',v1i)+"muss jedoch mindestens "+v2+" ergeben. Danke!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(16,ErrBegTxt(flg,'it',v1i)+"numero totale deve essere uguale o maggiore a "+v2+". Grazie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(10,ErrBegTxt(flg,'es',v1i)+"total debe ser igual o superior a "+v2+". Muchas gracias!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(22,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"deve ser igual ou maior do que "+v2+". Obrigado/a!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(20,ErrBegTxt(flg,'no',v1i)+"må være større enn eller tilsvare "+v2+". Takk!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(6,ErrBegTxt(flg,'da',v1i)+"skal være større end eller lig med "+v2+". Mange tak!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(29,ErrBegTxt(flg,'sv',v1i)+"måste vara större än eller lika med "+v2+". Tack!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(31,ErrBegTxt(flg,'tr',v1i)+"en az veya tam olarak "+v2+" olmalidir. Tesekkür ederiz!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(18,ErrBegTxt(flg,'ko',v1i)+v2+" &#48372;&#45796; &#53356;&#44144;&#45208;  &#46041;&#46321;&#54644;&#50556; &#54633;&#45768;&#45796;. &#44048;&#49324;&#54633;&#45768;&#45796;!");

}
break;
 
case '!=':
 
if (v1!=v2){

RaiseError();

SetQuestionErrorMessage(9,ErrBegTxt(flg,'en',v1i)+"must be  equal to "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(54,ErrBegTxt(flg,'af',v1i)+"moet gelyk wees aan "+v2+". Dankie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(12,ErrBegTxt(flg,'fr',v1i)+"doit être égale à "+v2+". Merci!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(7,ErrBegTxt(flg,'de',v1i)+"muss jedoch gleich "+v2+". Danke!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(16,ErrBegTxt(flg,'it',v1i)+"deve corrispondere al "+v2+". Grazie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(10,ErrBegTxt(flg,'es',v1i)+"debe ser igual a "+v2+". Muchas gracias!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(22,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"deve ser igual a "+v2+". Obrigado/a!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(20,ErrBegTxt(flg,'no',v1i)+"må tilsvare "+v2+". Takk!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(6,ErrBegTxt(flg,'da',v1i)+"skal være lig med "+v2+". Mange tak!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(29,ErrBegTxt(flg,'sv',v1i)+"måste vara lika med "+v2+". Tack!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(31,ErrBegTxt(flg,'tr',v1i)+"tam olarak "+v2+" olmalidir. Tesekkür ederiz!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(18,ErrBegTxt(flg,'ko',v1i)+v2+" &#44284;&#40;&#50752;&#41; &#46041;&#46321;&#54644;&#50556;  &#54633;&#45768;&#45796;. &#44048;&#49324;&#54633;&#45768;&#45796;!");

}
break;
 
case '==':
 
if (v1==v2){
RaiseError();

SetQuestionErrorMessage(9,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"must not be equal to "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(54,ErrBegTxt(flg,'af',v1i)+"moet nie gelyk wees aan "+v2+". Dankie!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(12,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"must not be equal to "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(7,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"must not be equal to "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(16,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"must not be equal to "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(10,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"must not be equal to "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(22,ErrBegTxt(flg,'pt',v1i)+"must not be equal to "+v2+". Thank you!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(20,ErrBegTxt(flg,'no',v1i)+"må ikke tsilsvare "+v2+". Takk!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(6,ErrBegTxt(flg,'da',v1i)+"skal ikke være lig med "+v2+". Mange tak!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(29,ErrBegTxt(flg,'sv',v1i)+"får inte vara lika med "+v2+". Tack!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(31,ErrBegTxt(flg,'tr',v1i)+"suna esit olmayan bir rakam "+v2+" olmalidir. Tesekkür ederiz!");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(18,ErrBegTxt(flg,'ko',v1i)+v2+" &#44284;&#40;&#50752;&#41; &#46041;&#46321;&#54644;&#49436;&#45716;  &#50504;&#46121;&#45768;&#45796;. &#44048;&#49324;&#54633;&#45768;&#45796;!");

}
break;

}


}

function ErrBegTxt(flag,lng,q2)
{

/*Changes the beginning of the error msg depending on whether the question to be evaluated is a multi('the sum of your  answers is....') or an open ('your answer..') or an answer from a multi (label of answer...)*/

var begtx;

if (flag==1){

switch (lng){

/* if multi dispay this...*/

case 'af':
begtx = "Die totaal van u antwoorde is "+q2+". dit ";
return begtx;
break;

case 'en':
begtx = "The sum of your answers is "+q2+". It ";
return begtx;
break;

case 'fr':
begtx = "La somme de vos réponses est "+q2+". Elle ";
return begtx
break;

case 'de':
begtx = "Die Summe Ihrer Antworten ergibt "+q2+". Sie ";
return begtx
break;

case 'it':
begtx = "La somma delle Sue risposte è di "+q2+". Il ";
return begtx
break;

case 'es':
begtx = "El total de sus respuestas es "+q2+". Este ";
return begtx
break;

case 'pt':
begtx = "O total de suas respostas é de "+q2+". Ele ";
return begtx
break;

case 'no':
begtx = "Summen av svarene dine er "+q2+". Det ";
return begtx
break;

case 'da':
begtx = "Summen af dine svar er "+q2+". Den ";
return begtx
break;

case 'sv':
begtx = "Summan av dina svar är "+q2+". Den ";
return begtx
break;

case 'tr':
begtx = "Cevaplarinizin toplami "+q2+". Oysa ";
return begtx
break;

case 'ko':
begtx = "&#44480;&#54616;&#51032; &#45813;&#48320; &#54633;&#44228;&#45716; "+q2+" &#51077;&#45768;&#45796;. &#51060;  &#54633;&#44228;&#45716; ";
return begtx
break;

}

}


else

/*if opentext type question display:*/

{
var q2str; //stroe string value of q2
var fv1; //store f(que1) value

q2str = q2.toString(); 
fv1 = f(q2).label();

/* Message for specific question in a multi*/

if (q2str.match(/_/)) //evals to true if there is an underscore
{
return "&laquo;"+fv1+"&raquo; "; //HtML special characters used for <<>>
}

/* Message for opentext*/

else
{

switch (lng){

case 'en':
return "Your answer ";
break;

case 'af':
return "U antwoord ";
break;

case 'fr':
return "Votre réponse ";
break;

case 'de':
return "Ihre Antwort ";
break;

case 'it':
return "La Sua risposta ";
break;

case 'es':
return "Su respuesta ";
break;

case 'pt':
return "Sua resposta ";
break;

case 'no':
return "Svaret ditt ";
break;

case 'da':
return "Dit svar ";
break;

case 'sv':
return "Ditt svar ";
break;

case 'tr':
return "Cevabiniz ";
break;

case 'ko':
return "&#44480;&#54616;&#51032; &#45813;&#48320; ";
break;


}

}

}

}

/*-------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

function add100(fid)
{

/* Wrapper function which facilitates making multis add up too 100 */

var qu;

if(!fid)
{
qu=CurrentForm();
}
else
{
qu=fid;
}

compare(qu,'!=','100');

}

multireq
function multireq(min,max,qud)

/* 
Requires a multi question to have a minimum of "min" answers
qud is optional (only really used for 3D grids)
*/

{

var CurrF;

if (!qud)
{
CurrF=f(CurrentForm());
}
else
{
CurrF=f(qud);
}

var plural =""; //Default no plural for "answer" in error msg

if (!min || min==1)
{

min=1;

}

else
//add 's' to answer
{


var plural=langs('p'); //get plural from langs function



}



if (CurrF.size()<min)
{

RaiseError();
SetQuestionErrorMessage(9,"Please select a "+langs('min')+" of "+min+" answer"+plural+". Thank You!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(12,"Veuillez sélectionner "+min+" réponse"+plural+" au "+langs('min')+". Merci!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(7,"Bitte "+langs('min')+" "+min+" Antwort"+plural+" auswählen. Danke!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(16,"Selezionare un "+langs('min')+" di "+min+" risposte"+plural+". Grazie!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(10,"Sírvase seleccionar un "+langs('min')+" de "+min+" respuesta"+plural+". ¡Gracias!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(22,"Selecione por favor um "+langs('min')+" de "+min+" respostas"+plural+". Obrigado/a!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(29,"Välj ett "+langs('min')+" om "+min+" svar"+plural+". Tack så mycket.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(31,"Lütfen en "+langs('min')+" "+min+" cevap"+plural+" seçiniz. Tesekkür Ederiz!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(19,"Gelieve te selecteren minstens "+min+" antwoord"+plural+".");}

if (max)
{

if (CurrF.size()>max)
{

RaiseError();
SetQuestionErrorMessage(9,"Please select a "+langs('max')+" of "+max+" answer"+plural+". Thank You!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(12,"Veuillez sélectionner "+max+" réponse"+plural+" au "+langs('max')+". Merci!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(7,"Bitte "+langs('max')+" "+max+" Antwort"+plural+" auswählen. Danke!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(16,"Selezionare un "+langs('max')+" di "+max+" risposte"+plural+". Grazie!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(10,"Sírvase seleccionar un "+langs('max')+" de "+max+" respuesta"+plural+". ¡Gracias!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(22,"Selecione por favor um "+langs('max')+" de "+max+" respostas"+plural+". Obrigado/a!");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(29,"Välj ett "+langs('max')+" om "+max+" svar"+plural+". Tack så mycket.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(31,"Lütfen en "+langs('max')+" "+max+" cevap"+plural+" seçiniz. Tesekkür Ederiz!");

}

}


}

function langs(selector)
{

var clang=CurrentLang();

if (selector=='p') //Plural
{

switch (clang){

case '9':
return "s";
break;

case '12':
return "s";
break;

case '7':
return "en";
break;

case '16':
return "";
break;

case '10':
return "s";
break;

//Portugal
case '22':
return "s";
break;

//Sweden
case '29':
return "";
break;

//Turkey
case '31':
return "lar";
break;

//Dutch
case '19':
return "";
break;


//Default
default:
return "";

}

}

if (selector=='min') //minimum
{


switch (clang){

case '9':
return "minimum";
break;

case '12':
return "minimum";
break;

case '7':
return "mindestens";
break;

case '16':
return "minimo";
break;

case '10':
return "mínimo";
break;

case '22':
return "mínimo";
break;


case '29':
return "minimum";
break;


case '31':
return "az";
break;


case '19':
return "minstens";
break;



//Default
default:
return "minimum";
}

}

if (selector='max') //maximum
{


switch (clang){

case '9':
return "maximum";
break;

case '12':
return "maximum";
break;

case '7':
return "höchstens";
break;

case '16':
return "massimo";
break;

case '10':
return "máximo";
break;

//Portugal
case '22':
return "máximo";
break;

//Sweden
case '29':
return "maximum";
break;

//Turkey
case '31':
return "fazla";
break;

case '19':
return "maxten";
break;

//Default
default:
return "maximum";
}

}

}


more_scripts
//COPIES QUESTIONS
//EXAMPLE copy('q1','q1l')
/*
Copies data from an entire question (including all answers and other specified) to another question. Useful for copying questions out of a loop.
*/


function copy(from,to)
{

if (f(from).toBoolean()) //So  blank values are not copied in
{

var othf; //stores value if other 
var otht; //same

othf = from + "_98_Other";
otht = to + "_98_Other";

if (f(from).COMPOUND && f(to).COMPOUND){

var precodes=f(from).domainValues()
var i;

for(i in precodes){

f(to)[precodes[i]].set(f(from)[precodes[i]])

if (precodes[i]==98){
f(otht).set(f(othf));

}

}

}

if (f(from).OPEN && f(to).OPEN){

f(to).set(f(from))
}

if (f(from).CODED && f(to).CODED){

f(to).set(f(from))

if (f(from)==98){
f(otht).set(f(othf));
}

}

}

}

function loopcopy(quad)
{

/* Wrapper function : FACILITATES COPYING QUESTIONS OUT OF LOOPS, REQUIRES THAT THE QUESTION BE COPIED ENDS WITH l i.e. q7l --> q7

SCRIPTS MUST BE USED IN VALIDATION SCRIPT NODE, will not work otherwise

*/

var cform;

if (!quad)
{
cform = CurrentForm();
}
else
{
cform=quad;
}

copy(cform ,cform.substring(0,cform.length-1));

}




Masking_Variation_1
// Created by Pasqualino, Jonathan and Billy
// Last revised: Feb 2007
// Functionality: masking function to be used when 0's are forced in a numeric multi (even in a 3D grid) or any other regular multi question

function multiMasking(qnum1)
{
   var v1 = f(qnum1);  // variable passed by the programmer in the function call
   var s = new Set();   // set of precodes passed back by this function
   var precodes = v1.domainValues(); //all precodes

   for(var i : int = 0;i<precodes.length;i++) 
   {
        var code = precodes[i];        
        if (v1[code].toNumber() >0)
        {
            s.add(code);
        } // end of if statement
   } // end of for loop
   return s; // return the set of precodes
} // end of function multiMasking


Masking_Variation_2
// Created by Pasqualino, Jonathan and Billy
// Last revised: Feb 2007
// Functionality: masking function to be used when 0's are NOT forced in a numeric multi (even in a 3D grid) or any other regular multi question

function multiMaskingB(qnum1)
{
   var v1 = f(qnum1);   // variable passed by the programmer in the function call
   var s = new Set();   // set of precodes passed back by this function
   var precodes = v1.domainValues(); //all precodes
   for(var i : int = 0;i<precodes.length;i++) 
   {
        var code = precodes[i];
        if (v1[code].toBoolean())
        {
            s.add(code);
        } // end of if statement
   } // end of for loop
   return s; // return the set of precodes
} // end of function multiMaskingB


CommonFunctions
/*
* Author - Coremind 
* Date Created - 30th March 2007
* Script node description: This script contains the functions used commonly throughout the survey.
*/


//Used for setting the status to Screened if the respondent is screened out.
function ScreenedOut()
{
SetStatus('screened');
Redirect("http://www.pslgroup.com",false);
}

//Used for setting the status to QuotaFull.
function QuotaFull()
{
SetStatus("quotafull");
Redirect("http://www.pslgroup.com",false);
}

//Used for setting the status to Complete.
function SurveyComplete()
{
SetStatus("complete");
Redirect("http://www.pslgroup.com",false);
}

//Info for Screened out respondents.
function InfoTermination()
{
return "<center><br><br>Thank you for taking part in the survey. These are all the questions we have for you.<br><br><br></center>";
}

//Thank you info if the respondent completes the survey.
function InfoTerminationComplete()
{
return "<center><br><br>Thank you for taking part in the survey.<br><br><br></center>";
}



// VALIDATION FOR OTHER SPECIFY BOX 3DGRID AND MULTI QUESTION.

function ChkOther(gID_Other,qID,qprecode) 
{
var form = f(qID);
var strTemp = gID_Other;

if(f(qID).inc(qprecode) && strTemp=="")
{
RaiseError();
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please provide a response in the 'specify box' if the option is chosen.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, en el caso que elija la opción, introduzca una respuesta en la casilla específica.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Inserisca una risposta nella casella specificare se seleziona la relativa opzione.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez fournir une réponse dans la case 'Préciser' si l'option a été sélectionnée");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte geben Sie eine Antwort in dem Feld 'bitte angeben', wenn Sie diese Option gewählt haben.");

}

if(strTemp!="" && !(f(qID).inc(qprecode)))
{
RaiseError();
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please select the option if you provide a response in the 'specify box'.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez sélectionner l'option si une réponse a été fournie dans la case 'Préciser'.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Selezioni lopzione corrispondente se inserisce una risposta nella casella specificare.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte waehlen Sie die Option, wenn Sie eine Antwort in dem Feld 'bitte angeben' gegeben haben.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, seleccione la opción en la casilla específica en el caso que introduzca una respuesta.");

}
}


set_ErrorMessages
/* 
*  Author: Coremind
*  Date created: March 30, 2007
*  Script node description:  This function has been created to Store the Error messages for the entire Questionnaire.
*/

function getValid(num:String)
{
   RaiseError();
   switch(num)
   {

          case 's7': 
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please make sure that the sum total of all your answers equals to "+ f('s5')['01'].get()+".");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte stellen Sie sicher, dass die Summe Ihrer Antworten "+ f('s5')['01'].get() +" ergibt.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez vous assurer que la somme de vos réponses est égale à "+ f('s5')['01'].get() +".");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, asegúrese de que la suma total de todas sus respuestas sea igual a "+ f('s5')['01'].get() +".");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Si assicuri che il totale di tutte le Sue risposte sia pari a"+ f('s5')['01'].get() +".");
               break;

          case 's8': 
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please make sure that the sum total of all your answers equals to 100.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte stellen Sie sicher, dass die Summe Ihrer Antworten 100 ergibt.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez vous assurer que la somme de vos réponses est égale à 100.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, asegúrese de que la suma total de todas sus respuestas sea igual a 100.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Si assicuri che il totale di tutte le Sue risposte sia pari a 100");
           break;

          case 'q1_5option':
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please provide a response in the 'specify box' if you provide a value in other.");
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte geben Sie eine Antwort in dem Feld 'bitte angeben', wenn Sie diese Option gewählt haben.");

                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, en el caso que elija la opción, introduzca una respuesta en la casilla específica.");
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Inserisca una risposta nella casella specificare se seleziona la relativa opzione.");
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez fournir une réponse dans la case 'Préciser' si l'option a été sélectionnée");
            break;

           case 'q1_5other':
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please provide a value greater than '0' in the other option if you provide a response in the 'specify box' OR delete the response in the specify box if its irrelevant.");
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte geben Sie einen Wert größer als 0 bei der Option Andere an, wenn Sie in dem Feld bitte angeben eine Antwort geben ODER löschen Sie die Antwort in dem Feld bitte angeben, wenn diese nicht relevant ist.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Si prega di fornire un valore superiore a 0 nellopzione altro nel caso abbia fornito una risposta nella casella si prega di specificare OPPURE di cancellare la risposta nella casella si prega di specificare se la ritenesse irrilevante.");
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, facilítenos una cifra mayor que '0' en la opción 'otra' si ha dado una respuesta en la casilla 'especifique', O borre la respuesta de la casilla 'especifique' si es irrelevante.");
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez fournir une valeur supérieure à '0' pour l'option 'autre' si vous avez fourni une réponse dans la case 'préciser' OU effacez la réponse de la case 'préciser' si celle-ci n'a pas lieu d'être");
            break;

         case 'q1_6both':
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please do not select 'I dont have any of these patients / I refer these patients to other physicians' if you specify some value in the text boxes of the same column.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte wählen Sie nicht Ich habe keine dieser Patienten / Ich überweise diese Patienten an andere Ärzte wenn Sie in den Textfeldern der gleichen Spalte einen Wert angeben.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Si prega di non selezionare 'Non ho alcun paziente di questo tipo / Invio questi pazienti ad un altro specialista nel caso abbia specificato dei valori nella casella del testo della stessa colonna.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, no elija 'no tengo ninguno de esos pacientes/derivo esos pacientes a otros médicos' si ha indicado alguna cifra en las casillas de texto de la misma columna.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez ne pas sélectionner 'Je n'ai aucun patients de ce type/ j'adresse ces patients à d'autres médecins' si vous avez fourni une valeur dans l'une ou plusieurs des cases de cette colonne.");
         break;

          case 'q1_6none':
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please review your responses, one or more columns require further input.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte sehen Sie sich Ihre Antworten erneut an. Eine oder mehrere Spalten erfordern weitere Angaben.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez revoir vos réponses, une ou plusieurs rangées nécessite(nt) dêtre remplie(s).");

          break;

          case 'q5_2':

getSum
/* 
*  Author: Coremind
*  Date created: March 30, 2007
*  Script node description:  This function has been created to calculate the sum of all the answers
*/

function getSum(qID)
{
var precodes,i,sum,code,tempVal

var form=f(qID)
precodes = form.domainValues(); //array with all precodes
i=0;
sum=0;

while(i<precodes.length)
{
code = precodes[i]; //current precode

//calculate the sum for one row:
tempVal=form[code].toNumber();

if (tempVal>0)
sum = sum + form[code].toNumber();
else
sum=sum+0
i++;
}

return sum
}


CheckOther
/* 
*  Author: Coremind
*  Date created: March 30, 2007
*  Script node description:  This function has been created to check for Other specify box if value greater than 0
*/

// VALIDATION FOR OTHER SPECIFY BOX 3DGRID AND MULTI OPEN END QUESTION.

function CheckOther(gID,qID,qprecode) 
{
var form = f(qID);
var strTemp=gID;

if(f(qID)[qprecode].toNumber()>0 && strTemp=="")
{
RaiseError();
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please provide a response in the 'specify box' if you provide a value greater than 0 in other.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte geben Sie in dem Feld bitte angeben eine Antwort ein, wenn Sie bei Andere einen Wert größer als 0 eingegeben.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Si prega di fornire una risposta nella casella si prega di specificare nel caso abbia fornito un valore maggiore di 0 nella voce 'altro'");

              SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, en el caso que elija la opción, introduzca una respuesta en la casilla específica.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez fournir une réponse dans la case 'Préciser' si l'option a été sélectionnée");


}

if(strTemp!="" && !(f(qID).inc(qprecode)))
{
RaiseError();
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please provide a value in the other option if you provide a response in the 'specify box'.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte geben Sie bei Andere einen Wert ein, wenn Sie im Feld bitte angeben eine Antwort geben.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Selezioni lopzione corrispondente se inserisce una risposta nella casella specificare.");

SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, facilítenos una cifra mayor que '0' en la opción 'otra' si ha dado una respuesta en la casilla 'especifique', O borre la respuesta de la casilla 'especifique' si es irrelevante.");
SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez fournir une valeur supérieure à '0' pour l'option 'autre' si vous avez fourni une réponse dans la case 'préciser' OU effacez la réponse de la case 'préciser' si celle-ci n'a pas lieu d'être");

}
}

setRandomNumber
// create a random number and set in X_1

// change this value to the (number of branches you need X 3) - 1
var seedNb = 14;

var random_num;
random_num = (Math.round((Math.random() * seedNb) + 1));
f('X_1').set(random_num);


branching
// Check the random number and set a value to Final
// this will be used for branching.
// 
// Ajust the number of IF statements to the number of branches you need
// also change the seedNb variable in setRandomNumber

// branch 1
if (f('X_1') =='1' || f('X_1') =='6' || f('X_1') =='11')
   f('Final').set('1'); 

// branch 2
if (f('X_1') =='2' || f('X_1') =='7' || f('X_1') =='12')
   f('Final').set('2'); 

// branch 3
if (f('X_1') =='3' || f('X_1') =='8' || f('X_1') =='13')
   f('Final').set('3'); 

// branch 4
if (f('X_1') =='4' || f('X_1') =='9' || f('X_1') =='14')
   f('Final').set('4'); 

// branch 5
if (f('X_1') =='5' || f('X_1') =='10' || f('X_1') =='15')
   f('Final').set('5');

   var redirLocation;

   else
      redirLocation = "http://" + host + path + qs + "&n=" + lang;

    location = redirLocation;
    }
</script>

sSpecialtyM
/* 
*  Author: Coremind
*  Date created: March 30, 2007
*  Script node description:  This node has been created to punch value in the hidden question SpecialtyM to present the relevant specialties in Specialty..

Gastroenterologist	31 Hepatologist	131 Infectious disease specialist	45 
Internal medicine specialist	152 Hepato-gastroenterologist	1001

United Kingdom	227 France	68 Germany	74 Italy	98 Spain	180

*/

f('SpecialtyM')['31'].set('1') // select gastroenterologist
f('SpecialtyM')['131'].set('1') // select Hepatologist
f('SpecialtyM')['45'].set('0') // select infectious disease
f('SpecialtyM')['152'].set('0') //select internal medicine
f('SpecialtyM')['1001'].set('0') //select hepato-gastroenterologist
f('SpecialtyM')['999'].set('1') //select other

if(f('Country').get()=='98') // Italy
{
f('SpecialtyM')['31'].set('1') // select gastroenterologist
f('SpecialtyM')['131'].set('1') // select Hepatologist
f('SpecialtyM')['45'].set('1') // select infectious disease
f('SpecialtyM')['152'].set('1') //select internal medicine
f('SpecialtyM')['1001'].set('0') //select hepato-gastroenterologist
f('SpecialtyM')['999'].set('1') //select other
}

if(f('Country').get()=='74') //Germany
{
f('SpecialtyM')['31'].set('1') // select gastroenterologist
f('SpecialtyM')['131'].set('1') // select Hepatologist
f('SpecialtyM')['45'].set('0') // select infectious disease
f('SpecialtyM')['152'].set('1') //select internal medicine
f('SpecialtyM')['1001'].set('0') //select hepato-gastroenterologist
f('SpecialtyM')['999'].set('1') //select other
}

if(f('Country').get()=='68') //France
{
f('SpecialtyM')['31'].set('1') // select gastroenterologist
f('SpecialtyM')['131'].set('1') // select Hepatologist
f('SpecialtyM')['45'].set('0') // select infectious disease
f('SpecialtyM')['152'].set('0') //select internal medicine
f('SpecialtyM')['1001'].set('1') //select hepato-gastroenterologist
f('SpecialtyM')['999'].set('1') //select other
}

Quota setup







sqQuotaH
/* 
*  Author: Coremind
*  Date created: April 13, 2007
*  Script node description:  This node has been created to punch value as per the quota condition in the hidden question qQuotaH for the countries UK, France and Spain.

*/

f('qQuotaH').set(null) //clear up old values if any

//UK punch quota if (S2a=1.or.2)
if(f('Country').get()=='227' && (f('Specialty').get()=='31' || f('Specialty').get()=='131'))
f('qQuotaH').set('01')

//france punch quota if (S2a=1.or.2.or.5)
if(f('Country').get()=='68' && (f('Specialty').get()=='31' || f('Specialty').get()=='131' || f('Specialty').get()=='1001' ))
f('qQuotaH').set('02')

//spain punch quota if (S2a=1.or.2)
if(f('Country').get()=='180' && (f('Specialty').get()=='31' || f('Specialty').get()=='131' ))
f('qQuotaH').set('03')


sqQuota2H
/* 
*  Author: Coremind
*  Date created: March 30, 2007
*  Script node description:  This node has been created to punch value as per the quota condition in the hidden question qQuotaH for the country Germany.

*/

f('qQuota2H').set(null) //clear up old values if any


if(f('Country').get()=='74')
{
 //punch quota if (S2a=1.or.2).AND.(S2b=3.or.4.or.5)
 if((f('Specialty').get()=='31' || f('Specialty').get()=='131') && (f('s2b').get()=='03' || f('s2b').get()=='04' || f('s2b').get()=='05'))
 f('qQuota2H').set('01');

 //punch quota if (S2a=1.or.2).AND.(S2b=1.or.2)
 if((f('Specialty').get()=='31' || f('Specialty').get()=='131') && (f('s2b').get()=='01' || f('s2b').get()=='02' ))
 f('qQuota2H').set('02');

 //punch quota if (S2a=4).AND.(S2b=1.or.2)
 if((f('Specialty').get()=='152') && (f('s2b').get()=='01' || f('s2b').get()=='02'))
 f('qQuota2H').set('03');

 //punch quota if (S2a=4).AND.(S2b=3 or 4 or 5)
 if((f('Specialty').get()=='152') && (f('s2b').get()=='03' || f('s2b').get()=='04' || f('s2b').get()=='05'))
 f('qQuota2H').set('04');

}


sqQuota3H
/* 
*  Author: Coremind
*  Date created: March 30, 2007
*  Script node description:  This node has been created to punch value as per the quota condition in the hidden question qQuotaH for the countries ITALY.

*/

f('qQuota3H').set(null) //clear up old values if any


if(f('Country').get()=='98')
{
 //punch quota if (S2a=1.or.2)
 if((f('Specialty').get()=='31' || f('Specialty').get()=='131'))
 f('qQuota3H').set('01');

sendReceipt
/*
Description: Sends a participation receipt by email to the respondant
Date Created: 11/02/04
Created By: Neil Doshi(neild@pslgroup.com)
Last Modified: 11/15/04 by EC
*/


//Only process if list is a certain type


if (f('BG_Source')==1||f('BG_Source')==3||f('BG_Source')==4||f('BG_Source')==5||f('BG_Source')==11)

{

//Email Content
var msg;
var subj;

//map mailing info vars from BG variables

var fname=f('HonoMailS_1');
var lname=f('HonoMailS_2');
var email=f('HonoMailS_3');
var address1=f('HonoMails_4');
var city=f('HonoMailS_5');
var state=f('HonoMailS_6');
var country=f('HonoMailS_7');
var zip=f('HonoMailS_8');
var personid=f('BG_personid'); 
var projnumber=f('BG_ProjectNumber');
var servicename=f('BG_Service').valueLabel(); //Medefield or PSLResearch

//Set msg variables

var fulladdress=fname+" "+lname+"\n"+address1+"\n"+city+","+state+"\n"+country+"\n"+zip;

var confirmationnum = projnumber+"-"+personid;

var hono=f('BG_HonoAmount_Screened')+" "+f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel()+" "+f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel();


//build msg of email:


switch (CurrentLang()) {

case 12: //French

if (f('BG_HonoType')==1)
{
//Cheque

hono="l'adresse suivant un "+f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel()+" dune valeur de "+f('BG_HonoAmount_Screened')+" "+f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel();
}
else
{
hono="cette adresse électronique un chèque-cadeau dune valeur de "+f('BG_HonoAmount_Screened')+" "+f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel()+" in "+f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel();
}


subj = servicename+" confirmation de votre participation "+projnumber

msg = servicename+" vous remercie pour votre participation à cette étude.\n\nEn remerciement de votre participation, vous recevrez à "+hono+" dici 4 à 6 semaines :\n\n"+fulladdress+"\n\nVeuillez utiliser le NUMERO DE CONFIRMATION suivant si vous avez des questions concernant cette étude ou votre chèque-cadeau : "+confirmationnum+". Si vous avez des questions, nhésitez pas à nous contacter à ladresse suivante :\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nCordialement,\nLaura Malett\nResponsable de la recherche\n"

break;
   
case 7: //German

subj = servicename+" Teilnahmebestätigung "+projnumber

msg = servicename+" dankt Ihnen für Ihre erfolgreiche Teilnahme an dieser Studie.\n\nAls Dankeschön für Ihre Teilnahme werden wir in den nächsten 4-6 Wochen einen Geschenkgutschein in Höhe von  "+hono+" an die folgende E-Mail-Adresse schicken:\n\n"+fulladdress+"\n\nGeben Sie bei Anfragen im Zusammenhang mit der Studie oder der Übermittlung Ihrer Aufwandsentschädigung bitte die folgende KENNNUMMER an: "+confirmationnum+". Bei Fragen können Sie uns unter der folgenden Adresse erreichen:\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nMit freundlichen Grüßen,\nLaura Malett\nResearch Coordinator\n"

break;

case 10: //Spanish

subj = "Confirmación de participación "+projnumber+" de "+servicename

msg = servicename+" agradece su participación en el estudio.\n\nComo muestra de agradecimiento, en las próximas 4-6 semanas recibirá una gratificación de "+hono+" en la dirección siguiente:\n\n"+fulladdress+"\n\nPor favor, cite el NÚMERO DE CONFIRMACIÓN siguiente si tiene alguna pregunta sobre el estudio o sobre el pago de su gratificación: "+confirmationnum+". Si desea hacernos alguna consulta, póngase en contacto con nosotros a través de:\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nCordialmente,\nLaura Malett\nCoordinadora de estudios\n"

break;

case 16: //Italian

subj = "Conferma n. "+projnumber+" di partecipazione ad una ricerca di "+servicename

msg = servicename+" La ringrazia per aver partecipato attivamente a questo studio.\n\nIn considerazione del tempo da Lei dedicatoci, nelle prossime 4-6 settimane Le invieremo un compenso di $"+hono+" al seguente indirizzo:\n\n"+fulladdress+"\n\n Se desidera ricevere delucidazioni sullo studio o sul pagamento del Suo compenso, La invitiamo ad utilizzare il seguente NUMERO DI CONFERMA: "+confirmationnum+". Per ulteriori informazioni, ci contatti allindirizzo:\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nCordiali saluti.\n\nLaura Malett\nCoordinatrice della Ricerca\n"

break;

default:

//hono text changes depending on honotype

if (f('BG_HonoType')==1)
{
//Cheque
hono=f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel()+" of "+f('BG_HonoAmount_Screened')+" "+f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel();
}
else
{
hono="of "+f('BG_HonoAmount_Screened')+" "+f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel()+" in "+f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel();
}

subj = servicename+" participation confirmation "+projnumber

msg =servicename+" thanks you for your successful participation in this study.\n\nIn appreciation of your time an honorarium "+hono+" will be sent to you in the next 4-6 weeks to this address:\n\n"+fulladdress+"\n\nPlease use the following CONFIRMATION NUMBER if you have any questions about the study or payment of your honorarium: "+confirmationnum+". Should you have any queries, you can contact us at:\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nBest Regards,\nLaura Malett\nResearch Coordinator\n"


} 


//send mail:
SendMail("lauram@pslresearch.com",f('HonoMailS_3'),subj,msg);

//Verification that confirmation email has been sent
f('mail_sentS').set(1) 


} //THE END

</b>Leider haben wir schon eine ausreichende Anzahl Teilnehmer, deshalb können Sie diesmal nicht die komplette Umfrage ausfüllen. Wir bitten um Entschuldigung und hoffen, auch in Zukunft auf Ihre Mithilfe für unsere Studien zählen zu können.
<br><br>


</b>Vi har uppnått vårt behövliga antal besvarare, därmed kan du inte besvara hela frågeformuläret. Vi ber om ursäkt för orsakade problem och vi hoppas att du kommer att delta i våra kommande studier.  <br><br>


</b>U kunt niet de gehele vragenlijst invullen omdat wij het gewenste aantal antwoorden reeds ontvangen hebben. Wij bieden onze excuses aan voor het ongemak en hopen dat bereid bent aan toekomstige enquêtes deel te nemen.
<br><br>


</b><br><br>Agradecemos o tempo dispendido por V. em responder às nossas perguntas. Nesta oportunidade, por motivos de amostragem, não lhe pediremos para responder ao questionário completo. Novamente, nossos agradecimentos. Esperamos que possa participar conosco de futuras pesquisas.


</b>Abbiamo ottenuto il numero di risposte richiesto, per cui non potrà completare lintero questionario. Ci scusiamo per il disturbo e auspichiamo che, in futuro, possa partecipare ad altre nostre ricerche.
<br><br>


</b>Nous avons atteint notre nombre de réponses requis, par conséquent, il ne vous sera pas possible de compléter la totalité du questionnaire.  Nous vous prions de nous excuser pour votre dérangement et espérons quil vous sera possible de participer à de futures  études avec nous.  
<br><br>


</b>Hemos llegado al número requerido de respuestas y, por consiguiente, no podrá completar todo el cuestionario. Le pedimos disculpas por los inconvenientes y esperamos contar con su participación en nuestros estudios futuros.

gq1_4




<bR><br>
For reasons beyond their control doctors like yourself arent always able to prescribe the medications they would like to. 
<bR><br>
Please look at the following list of reasons and indicate whether or not they apply to each of the drugs you could or do use.
<bR><br>


<br><br>
Aus Gründen, die außerhalb der Kontrolle der Ärzte liegen, ist es Ärzten wie Ihnen nicht immer möglich das von ihnen gewünschte Medikament zu verordnen.
<br><br>
Bitte sehen Sie sich die folgende Liste mit Gründen an, und geben Sie an, ob diese auf die jeweiligen Medikamente zutreffen, die Sie einsetzen (könnten).
<br><br>








<br><Br>Per motivi al di fuori della propria portata, non è sempre possibile per i medici prescrivere i farmaci desiderati. 
<br><Br>

<br><br>

for(i=0;i<myprecodes.length;i++)
{
  code=myprecodes[i]
  f('q2_9_H')[code].set('0') // clear up old values in the hidden mask question.
}

myprecodes=f('q1_2').categories(); //get all selected values in Q1_2

for(i=0;i<myprecodes.length;i++)
{
  code=myprecodes[i]
  f('q2_9_H')[code].set('1') //select option
}

if(f('q2_4').inc('05')) f('q2_9_H')['05'].set('1'); // if tenofovir aware at q2.4 select in 2_9m

var mycounter,i;
mycounter=0;
var code;

var myprecodes=f('q2_9_H').domainValues();

for(i=0;i<myprecodes.length;i++)
{
 code=myprecodes[i];
 f('q2_9M')[code].set('0');
 f('q2_9aM')[code].set('0');
}
myprecodes=f('q2_9_H').categories();

for(i=0;i<myprecodes.length;i++)
{
code=myprecodes[i];

if(mycounter>=0 && mycounter<=4)
{
 f('q2_9M')[code].set('1')
 mycounter++;
}
else if(mycounter>4)
{
 f('q2_9aM')[code].set('1')
 mycounter++;
}

}

<br><br>
Bitte stellen Sie sicher, dass Sie alle Medikamente angeben, die Ihrer Meinung nach stark mit der jeweiligen Eigenschaft assoziiert werden.

var precodes = f("q2_9a").domainValues(); //array with all precodes
var i : int = 0;
var correctSum : Boolean = true; //Boolean variable. Will be set to false when a sum is not correct
while(i<precodes.length && correctSum)
 {
  var code = precodes[i]; //current precode
  //calculate the sum for one row:
  if((f('q2_9a')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9b')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9d')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9e')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9f')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9g')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9None')[code].toBoolean()  ) && f('q2_9dk')[code].toBoolean() )
   {
   RaiseError();
   SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please make sure you have not selected 'Don't know' with any other answers.");
   SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte stellen Sie sicher, dass Sie nicht 'Weiß nicht' zur gleichen Zeit wie eine andere Antwort gewählt haben.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Si assicuri di non aver selezionato Non so/<br>incerto' nel caso abbia già selezionato altre risposte.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, asegúrese de que no ha seleccionado la opción 'No lo sé / no estoy seguro/a' a la vez que alguna otra respuesta.");   
   SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez vous assurer que vous n'avez pas sélectionné l'option 'Ne sais pas / indécis(e)' pour l'une des autres réponses.");

}

  if((f('q2_9a')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9b')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9d')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9e')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9f')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9g')[code].toBoolean() || f('q2_9dk')[code].toBoolean()  ) && f('q2_9None')[code].toBoolean() )
   {
   RaiseError();
   getValid('q2_9None')
   }

  i++;
 }


var myprecodes=f('q2_9a').domainValues();

for(i=0;i<myprecodes.length;i++)
{
code=myprecodes[i];
if(!f('q2_9a').inc(code) && !f('q2_9b').inc(code) && !f('q2_9d').inc(code) && !f('q2_9e').inc(code) && !f('q2_9f').inc(code) && !f('q2_9g').inc(code) && !f('q2_9None').inc(code) && !f('q2_9dk').inc(code))
 getValid('q2_9')

}

Logra una supresión rápida y sostenida del ADN del VHB en suero hasta niveles indetectables.
















Demonstrates a high genetic barrier to resistance among nucleoside-naive patients
Weist bei nukleosid-naiven Patienten eine hohe genetische Resistenzbarriere auf



Ha dimostrato unelevata barriera genetica alle resistenze nei pazienti naïve agli analoghi  nucleosidici
Présente une barrière génétique élevée à la résistance chez les patients naïfs aux inhibiteurs nucléosidiques
Demuestra una alta barrera genética a la resistencia entre los pacientes que nunca habían sido tratados con nucleósidos.

var correctSum : Boolean = true; //Boolean variable. Will be set to false when a sum is not correct
while(i<precodes.length && correctSum)
 {
  var code = precodes[i]; //current precode

  if((f('q3_1a1')[code].toBoolean() || f('q3_1a2')[code].toBoolean() || f('q3_1a3')[code].toBoolean() ||  f('q3_1a4')[code].toBoolean() || f('q3_1aNone')[code].toBoolean()) && (f('q3_1adk')[code].toBoolean() )  )
   {
   RaiseError();
   SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please make sure you have not selected 'Don't know' with any other answers.");
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte stellen Sie sicher, dass Sie nicht Weiß nicht/nicht sicher zur gleichen Zeit wie eine andere Antwort gewählt haben.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.it,"Si assicuri di non aver selezionato Non so/<br>incerto' nel caso abbia già selezionato altre risposte.");
                SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.es,"Por favor, asegúrese de que no ha seleccionado la opción 'No lo sé / no estoy seguro/a' a la vez que alguna otra respuesta.");
   SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez vous assurer que vous n'avez pas sélectionné l'option 'Ne sais pas / indécis(e)' pour l'une des autres réponses.");



   }

  if((f('q3_1a1')[code].toBoolean() || f('q3_1a2')[code].toBoolean() || f('q3_1a3')[code].toBoolean() ||  f('q3_1a4')[code].toBoolean() ||  f('q3_1adk')[code].toBoolean() ) && (f('q3_1aNone')[code].toBoolean() )  )
   {
   getValid('q2_9None')
    }

  if(!f('q3_1a1')[code].toBoolean() && !f('q3_1a2')[code].toBoolean() && !f('q3_1a3')[code].toBoolean() && !f('q3_1a4')[code].toBoolean() && !f('q3_1adk')[code].toBoolean() && !f('q3_1aNone')[code].toBoolean() )
   {
   RaiseError();
   SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.en,"Please make sure you have selected an answer for '"+f('q3_1a1')[code].label()+"'.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.de,"Bitte stellen Sie sicher, das Sie in jeder Reihe eine Antwort gewählt haben.");
               SetQuestionErrorMessage(LangIDs.fr,"Veuillez fournir une réponse pour chaque ligne.");

   }

  i++;
 }

if(f('q2_4').inc('05')) // || f('q3_2f')['01'].toNumber()>0)
f('q3_4M')['02'].set('1') //select tenofovir

q4_1




<br><br>
For each of the following statements, please indicate your level of agreement or disagreement, where 1 means you strongly disagree and 5 means you strongly agree
<bR><Br>


<br><br>Bitte geben Sie bei jeder der folgenden Aussagen an, inwieweit Sie ihnen zustimmen oder diese ablehnen, wobei 1 bedeutet Sie lehnen sie stark ab und 5, dass Sie ihr stark zustimmen.<br><br>








<br><br>Per ciascuna delle seguenti affermazioni, indici in che misura è daccordo o in disaccordo. Usi una scala da 1 a 5 in cui 1 indica che Lei è fortemente in disaccordo e 5 indica che è fortemente daccordo<br><br>


<br><br>
Sur une échelle de 1 à 5 sur laquelle 1 signifie pas du tout daccord et 5 signifie tout à fait daccord, veuillez indiquer dans quelle mesure vous êtes daccord ou non avec les affirmations suivantes
<br><br>


<br><br>Por favor, indique hasta qué punto está de acuerdo o en desacuerdo con cada una de las siguientes declaraciones. 1 significa que está muy en desacuerdo y 5 que está muy de acuerdo.<Br><br>








I initiate first-line therapy with the product I believe has the most impact on viral load reduction
Ich initiiere eine First-Line Therapie mit dem Produkt, welches meiner Ansicht nach die größte Wirkung auf die Viruslastreduktion hat 



Inizio la terapia di prima linea con il farmaco che ritengo abbia il maggiore impatto sulla riduzione della carica virale
Jinstaure le traitement de première intention avec le produit que jestime avoir limpact le plus fort sur la réduction de la charge virale 
Inicio la terapia de primera línea con el producto que creo que tiene el mayor impacto en la reducción de la carga viral.
















I believe that HBV resistance can be easily managed
Ich glaube, dass eine HBV-Resistenz leicht handhabbar ist



Ritengo che la resistenza dellHBV possa essere facilmente gestita 
Je pense que la résistance du VHB peut être aisément gérée 
Creo que es fácil tratar la resistencia del VHB.
















I believe that HBV should be treated aggressively
Ich glaube, dass HBV aggressiv behandelt werden sollte 



Ritengo che lHBV dovrebbe essere trattata aggressivamente 
Je pense que le VHB devrait être traité de manière agressive 
Creo que el VHB debería tratarse de modo agresivo. 
















Rapid viral load reduction leads to greater treatment success
Eine schnelle Reduktion der Viruslast führt zu einem größeren Behandlungserfolg 



Una rapida riduzione della carica virale porta ad un maggiore successo terapeutico 
Une réduction rapide de la charge virale assure un meilleur succès thérapeutique 
Una reducción rápida de la carga viral conduce a un mayor éxito del tratamiento.
















I believe that impacting viral load is the best way to slow HBV disease progression
Ich glaube, dass ein Einwirken auf die Viruslast der beste Weg ist, die HBV Krankheitsprogression zu verlangsamen



Ritengo che riuscire ad avere un impatto sulla carica virale sia il modo migliore per rallentare la progressione della malattia da HBV 
Je pense quagir sur la charge virale est le meilleur moyen de ralentir la progression de la maladie liée au VHB 
Creo que tener un impacto en la carga viral es la mejor manera de ralentizar la progresión de la hepatitis B. 
















I always discuss viral load levels with my patients
Ich bespreche mit meinen Patienten immer den Stand der Viruslast 



Discuto sempre dei livelli della carica virale con i miei pazienti 
Je discute toujours du niveau de la charge virale avec mes patients 
Siempre comento los niveles de carga viral con mis pacientes.
















Combination therapy with a nucleoside and a nucleotide is the future of HBV treatment
Kombinationstherapie mit einem Nukleosid und einem Nukleotid ist die Zukunft der HBV Behandlung 



La terapia in associazione con un nucleosidico e un nucleotidico rappresenta il futuro per il trattamento dellHBV 
Lassociation dun inhibiteur nucléosidique et dun inhibiteur nucléotidique constitue lavenir de la prise en charge du VHB
La terapia de combinación con un nucleósido y un nucleótido es el futuro del tratamiento del VHB.
















My greatest challenge in treating HBV is a therapy's propensity to induce HBV resistance
Meine größte Herausforderung bei der Behandlung des HBV ist die Tendenz der Therapie, eine HBV-Resistenz hervorzurufen 



La maggiore difficoltà nel trattamento dellHBV è la tendenza della terapia a creare resistenza allHBV 
Le plus important défi auquel je suis confronté(e) dans le traitement du VHB est la tendance naturelle du traitement à induire une résistance au VHB 
El mayor desafío al que me enfrento al tratar el VHB es que la terapia sea propensa a inducir resistencia del VHB.
















Sustained HBV DNA reduction is a sign that Hep B antiviral treatment is working
Eine anhaltende HBV-DNA-Reduktion ist ein Anzeichen dafür, dass die antivirale Hep B Behandlung wirkt



La riduzione sostenuta dellHBV DNA è un segno che il trattamento antivirale per lepatite B sta funzionando 
Une réduction soutenue de lADN du VHB est un signe que le traitement contre le virus de l'hépatite B est efficace 
Una reducción sostenida del ADN del VHB es una señal de que el tratamiento antiviral para la hepatitis B está funcionando.
















It is worthwhile to treat patients with normal ALT levels
Es lohnt sich, Patienten mit normalen ALT-Werten zu behandeln 



È utile trattare i pazienti che presentano livelli normali di ALT 
Il y a un intérêt à traiter un patient présentant des taux d'ALAT normaux 
Merece la pena tratar a los pacientes que tienen niveles normales de ALT. 
















I prefer to wait for colleagues to report their experiences, before I trial a new (HBV) therapy agent
Ich bevorzuge es zu warten, bis meine Kollegen Ihre Erfahrungen mitteilen, bevor ich ein neues (HBV) Präparat ausprobiere 



Preferisco aspettare che altri colleghi riferiscano le proprie esperienze, prima di provare un nuovo agente per la terapia dellHBV 
Je préfère attendre que mes collègues me fassent part de leurs expériences avant dessayer un nouveau traitement contre le VHB 
Prefiero esperar a que mis compañeros informen sus experiencias antes de probar yo mismo un nuevo agente terapéutico (para el VHB).

*  Author: Coremind
*  Date created: April 23, 2007
*  Script node description:  Punch values in q5_9_03M  as per country for masking values in q5_9.

f('q5_9_03M')['01'].set('1') //select AASLD 01
f('q5_9_03M')['02'].set('1') //select EASL 02
f('q5_9_03M')['09'].set('1') //select Other 08
f('q5_9_03M')['10'].set('1') //select None 09

if(f('Country').get()=='227') //if UK
{
f('q5_9_03M')['03'].set('1') //select NICE 03
f('q5_9_03M')['04'].set('1') //select BASL 04
}
else
{
f('q5_9_03M')['03'].set('0') //de-select NICE 03
f('q5_9_03M')['04'].set('0') //de-select BASL 04
}

if(f('Country').get()=='98') //if italy
f('q5_9_03M')['05'].set('1') //select AISF 05
else
f('q5_9_03M')['05'].set('0') //de-select AISF 05

if(f('Country').get()=='74') //if germany
f('q5_9_03M')['06'].set('1') //select DEVS 06
else
f('q5_9_03M')['06'].set('0') //de-select DEVS 06

if(f('Country').get()=='180') //if spain
f('q5_9_03M')['07'].set('1') //select TBC 07
else
f('q5_9_03M')['07'].set('0') //de-select TBC 07

if(f('Country').get()=='68') //if france
f('q5_9_03M')['08'].set('1') //select TBC 08
else
f('q5_9_03M')['08'].set('0') //de-select TBC 08

f('Country')=='34' || f('Country')=='226' || f('Country')=='227' || f('Country')=='98' || f('Country')=='180' || f('Country')=='74' || f('Country')=='68'





setting_HP1
// setting the piping in for amazon and chapters
if( f('Country')=='34')
{
f('hp_pipe1').set('1');
f('hp_pipe2').set('1');
}
if( f('Country')=='226')
{
f('hp_pipe1').set('2');
f('hp_pipe2').set('2');
}
if( f('Country')=='227')
{
f('hp_pipe1').set('2');
f('hp_pipe2').set('3');
}
if( f('Country')=='68')
{
f('hp_pipe1').set('2');
f('hp_pipe2').set('4');
}
if( f('Country')=='74')
{
f('hp_pipe1').set('2');
f('hp_pipe2').set('5');
}
// setting the masking for each hono option for the country specific hono types
if( f('Country')=='34' || f('Country')=='226')
{
f('hpmask_01').set('1');
f('hpmask_02').set('0');
f('hpmask_03').set('1');
f('hpmask_04').set('1');
}
if( f('Country')=='68' || f('Country')=='74')
{
f('hpmask_01').set('0');
f('hpmask_02').set('0');
f('hpmask_03').set('1');
f('hpmask_04').set('1');
}

<br><br><br>
To demonstrate that we at HAB truly value the time you take to complete our surveys, we are working on improving the Honoraria Program available to you by developing an understanding of your reward preferences. <br><br>
<b>Our aim is to: <br><br></b>
 <ul>
<li>Offer you an Honoraria Program that best reflects the reward preferences of the majority of our community, in terms of how you would like to be compensated for your valuable time </li>
<li>Develop an Honoraria Program that will ensure you receive your rewards more rapidly</li>
  </ul>
The following question will help us determine your preferences for future rewards only, and does not reflect the honoraria offered for the current survey. <br><br>
<b>What is your Honoraria preference? </b><br><br>
Please rank your top 3 Reward Types; including any other reward ideas you may have that are not listed below. Please assign a 1 to your most favored reward type, a 2 for your second most preferred reward option, and 3 for your third most preferred option. <br><br>


<br><br><br>
Um Ihnen zu zeigen, dass wir hier bei HAB wirklich dankbar sind für Ihre Zeit und Hilfe bei der Vervollständigung unserer Befragungen, arbeiten wir an der Verbesserung des Honorarprogramms, indem wir versuchen mehr über Ihre Vorlieben für Belohnungen zu erfahren.
<br><br>
<b>Unser Ziel ist:<br><br></b>
<ul>
<li>Ihnen ein Honorarprogramm zu bieten, das die Vorlieben des größten Teils unserer Gemeinschaft widerspiegelt, d.h. wie Sie für Ihre wertvolle Zeit entlohnt werden möchten. </li>
<li>Ein Honorarprogramm zu entwickeln, das sicher stellt, dass Sie Ihre Belohnungen schneller erhalten. </li>
</ul>
Die folgende Frage hilft uns, Ihre Vorlieben für zukünftige Belohnungen zu bestimmen und hat keinen Einfluss auf die Belohnungen, die für diese aktuelle Befragung angeboten werden. <br><br>
<b>Welches Honorar bevorzugen Sie?</b><br><br>
Bitte wählen Sie Ihre 3 Lieblingsbelohnungen und ordnen Sie diese nach dem Grad Ihrer Bevorzugung. Schließen Sie auch solche Ideen mit ein die unten nicht aufgeführt sind. Bitte geben Sie Ihrem bevorzugten Belohnungstyp eine "1", der zweiten Wahl eine "2", und der dritten Wahl eine "3".<br><br>








<br><br><br>
A riprova che HAB riconosce il tempo prezioso che Lei dedica alle nostre indagini, ci stiamo preparando per migliorare il Programma di compensi che Le offriamo, definendo più precisamente le modalità di compenso che Lei preferisce. 
<br><br>
<b>Il nostro obiettivo è il seguente:<br><br></b>
<ul>
<li>Offrirle un programma di compensi che rispecchi al meglio le preferenze della maggioranza della nostra comunità di utenti, ossia definire le modalità di compenso per il tempo prezioso che Lei dedica alle indagini</li>
<li>Sviluppare un programma di compensi che possa consentirle di ricevere il compenso in tempi più brevi</li>
</ul>
La domanda che Le sottoponiamo di seguito ci consentirà di comprendere meglio le sue preferenze a partire dai prossimi compensi, non si riferisce al compenso previsto per la presente indagine.<br><br>
<b>Qualè la sua preferenza in termini di compenso?</b><br><br>
Indichi i primi tre tipi di compenso in ordine di preferenza; indichi altresì altri eventuali tipi di compenso che non sono inclusi nellelenco. Assegni il numero 1 al tipo di compenso che preferisce, 2 alla seconda opzione e 3 alla terza.<br><br>


<br><br><br>
L'équipe d'HAB apprécie vraiment le temps que vous consacrez à compléter ses étude(s), et en ce moment, afin d'améliorer les choix de récompenses qui vous sont offertes, nous aimerions connaître vos préférences sur ce sujet.<br><br>
<b>Notre objectif est de :<br><br></b>
 <ul>
<li>Vous offrir un programme de récompenses qui corresponde le plus possible aux préférences de la majorité d'entre-vous, pour ce qui est de la façon dont vous aimeriez être dédommagé(e)s pour le temps précieux que vous nous accordez. </li>
<li>Mettre en place un programme de récompenses qui nous permettra de vous faire parvenir vos récompenses plus rapidement. </li>
</ul>
La question qui suit nous permettra de mieux cerner vos préférences uniquement pour ce qui est des prochains étude(s) et ne s'applique pas aux choix offerts pour le présent étude. <br><br>
<b>Quels modes de récompense préférez-vous ?</b><br><br>
Veuillez sélectionner les 3 modes de récompenses que vous préféreriez, y compris d'autres idées de récompenses que vous pourriez nous proposer et qui ne figurent pas déjà sur la liste ci-dessous. Veuillez attribuer le chiffre "1" à votre tout premier choix de récompense, le chiffre "2" à votre second choix de récompense, et le chiffre "3" à votre troisième choix de récompense.<br><br>


<br><br><br>
Para demostrar que en HAB valoramos de verdad el tiempo que dedica a completar nuestros estudios, estamos trabajando para mejorar el Programa de Honorarios disponible fomentando el entendimiento de sus preferencias en cuanto a gratificaciones.
<br><br>
<b>Nuestro objetivo es:<br><br></b>
<ul>
<li>Ofrecerle un Programa de Honorarios que refleje mejor las gratificaciones preferidas por la mayoría de la comunidad en relación a la manera en que le gustaría ser recompensado por su valioso tiempo.</li>
<li>Desarrollar un Programa de Honorarios que asegure el recibo de sus gratificaciones más rápidamente.</li>
</ul>
La siguiente pregunta nos ayudará a determinar sus preferencias para futuras gratificaciones solamente.  La pregunta no refleja el honorario ofrecido para este estudio en particular.<br><br>
<b>¿Qué preferencia tiene en cuanto a Honorarios?</b><br><br>
Por favor, ordene sus 3 Tipos de Gratificación más importantes incluyendo cualquier otra idea sobre gratificaciones que pueda tener y que no esté en la lista. Por favor, asigne un 1 al tipo de gratificación que más prefiera, un 2 a su segunda opción más preferida y un 3 para su tercera opción más preferida. <br><br>

<br><br>Wenn sie fertig sind, bitte die Schaltfläche >> anklicken. <br><br>Vielen Dank.<br><br>

set_regionMask
var t;

// initialize the region question so it's empty
for (t = 1; t <= 117; t++)
  f('regionMaskH_' + t).set('0');

// UK
if (f('Country') == '227')
  {
  for (t = 1; t <= 49; t++)
    f('regionMaskH_' + t).set('1');
  }

// Germany
if (f('Country') == '74')
  {
  for (t = 50; t <= 65; t++)
    f('regionMaskH_' + t).set('1');
  }

// Italie
if (f('Country') == '98')
  {
  for (t = 66; t <= 82; t++)
    f('regionMaskH_' + t).set('1');
  }

// Spain
if (f('Country') == '180')
  {
  for (t = 83; t <= 94; t++)
    f('regionMaskH_' + t).set('1');
  f('regionMaskH_118').set('1');
  }

// France
if (f('Country') == '68')
  {
  for (t = 95; t <= 117; t++)
    f('regionMaskH_' + t).set('1');
  }

// set global regions hidden question
var t;

// London & SE
if (f('regionS2') >= 1 && f('regionS2') <= 13)
  f('globalRegion').set(1);

// Rest of England
if (f('regionS2') >= 14 && f('regionS2') <= 46)
  f('globalRegion').set(2);

// Scotland, Wales, NI
if (f('regionS2') >= 47 && f('regionS2') <= 49)
  f('globalRegion').set(3);

// East incl. Berlin
t = f('regionS2');
if (t == 50 || t == 51 || t == 57 || t ==  63 || t == 64 || t == 65)
  f('globalRegion').set(4);

// South germany
if (t == 52 || t ==  53 || t == 55 || t == 60 || t == 62)
  f('globalRegion').set(5);

// North germany
if (t == 54 || t == 56 || t == 58 || t == 59 || t == 61)
  f('globalRegion').set(6);

// North Italy
if (f('regionS2') >= 66 && f('regionS2') <= 73)
  f('globalRegion').set(7);

// Centre Italy
if (f('regionS2') >= 74 && f('regionS2') <= 78)
  f('globalRegion').set(8);

// South Italy
if (f('regionS2') >= 79 && f('regionS2') <= 82)
  f('globalRegion').set(9);

// Centre Spain
if (f('regionS2') >= 83 && f('regionS2') <= 86)
  f('globalRegion').set(10);

// North Spain
if (f('regionS2') >= 87 && f('regionS2') <= 90)
  f('globalRegion').set(11);

// South/East Spain
if (f('regionS2') >= 91 && f('regionS2') <= 94)
  f('globalRegion').set(12);

// Paris & RP
if (f('regionS2') >= 95 && f('regionS2') <= 96)
  f('globalRegion').set(13);

// North France
if (f('regionS2') >= 97 && f('regionS2') <= 108)
  f('globalRegion').set(14);

// South France
if (f('regionS2') >= 109 && f('regionS2') <= 117)
  f('globalRegion').set(15);

sendReceipt
/*
Description: Sends a participation receipt by email to the respondant
Date Created: 11/02/04
Created By: Neil Doshi(neild@pslgroup.com)
Last Modified: 11/15/04 by EC
Last Modified: 10/25/05 by PF

BG_HonoType
1 = check
2 = gift certificates from Amazon.co.uk 
3 = Amex

BG_Source
1 = Internal DB
3 = Jim Online
4 = Facta Research
5 = Medlist
11 = MMI
*/

//Only process if list is a certain type
if (f('BG_Source') == 1 || f('BG_Source') == 3 || f('BG_Source') == 4 || f('BG_Source') == 5 || f('BG_Source') == 11)
	{
	//Email Content
	var msg;
	var subj;

	//map mailing info vars from BG variables
	var fname = f('HonoMail_1');
	var lname = f('HonoMail_2');
	var emailAddress = f('HonoMail_3');
	var address1 = f('HonoMail_4');
	var city = f('HonoMail_5');
	var state = f('HonoMail_6');
	var country = f('HonoMail_7');
	var zip = f('HonoMail_8');
	var personid = f('BG_personid'); 
	var projnumber = f('BG_ProjectNumber');
	var servicename = f('BG_Service').valueLabel(); //Medefield or PSLResearch

	//Set msg variables
	if (f('BG_HonoType') == 2)
		var fulladdress = emailAddress;
	else
		var fulladdress = fname + " " + lname + "\n" + address1 + "\n" + city + "," + state + "\n" + country + "\n" + zip;
	var confirmationnum = projnumber + "-" + personid;
	var hono = f('BG_HonoAmount') + " " + f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel() + " " + f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel();

	//build msg of email:
	switch (CurrentLang()) 
		{
		case 12: //French

		//Cheque
		if (f('BG_HonoType') == 1)
			hono = "l'adresse suivant un " + f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel() + " dune valeur de " + f('BG_HonoAmount') + " " + f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel();
		else
			hono = "cette adresse électronique un chèque-cadeau dune valeur de " + f('BG_HonoAmount') + " " + f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel() + " in " + f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel();

		subj = servicename + " confirmation de votre participation " + projnumber;
		msg = servicename + " vous remercie pour votre participation à cette étude.\n\nEn remerciement de votre participation, vous recevrez à " + hono + " dici 6 à 8 semaines :\n\n"+fulladdress + "\n\nVeuillez utiliser le NUMERO DE CONFIRMATION suivant si vous avez des questions concernant cette étude ou votre chèque-cadeau : "+confirmationnum+". Si vous avez des questions, nhésitez pas à nous contacter à ladresse suivante :\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nCordialement,\nLaura Malett\nResponsable de la recherche\n";
		break;
   
		case 7: //German

		subj = servicename + " Teilnahmebestätigung " + projnumber;
		msg = servicename + " dankt Ihnen für Ihre erfolgreiche Teilnahme an dieser Studie.\n\nAls Dankeschön für Ihre Teilnahme werden wir in den nächsten 6-8 Wochen einen Geschenkgutschein in Höhe von  "+hono+" an die folgende E-Mail-Adresse schicken:\n\n"+fulladdress+"\n\nGeben Sie bei Anfragen im Zusammenhang mit der Studie oder der Übermittlung Ihrer Aufwandsentschädigung bitte die folgende KENNNUMMER an: "+confirmationnum+". Bei Fragen können Sie uns unter der folgenden Adresse erreichen:\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nMit freundlichen Grüßen,\nLaura Malett\nResearch Coordinator\n";
		break;

		case 10: //Spanish

		subj = "Confirmación de participación " + projnumber + " de " + servicename;
		msg = servicename + " agradece su participación en el estudio.\n\nComo muestra de agradecimiento, en las próximas 6-8 semanas recibirá una gratificación de "+hono+" en la dirección siguiente:\n\n"+fulladdress+"\n\nPor favor, cite el NÚMERO DE CONFIRMACIÓN siguiente si tiene alguna pregunta sobre el estudio o sobre el pago de su gratificación: "+confirmationnum+". Si desea hacernos alguna consulta, póngase en contacto con nosotros a través de:\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nCordialmente,\nLaura Malett\nCoordinadora de estudios\n";
		break;

		case 16: //Italian

		subj = "Conferma n. " + projnumber + " di partecipazione ad una ricerca di " + servicename;
		msg = servicename + " La ringrazia per aver partecipato attivamente a questo studio.\n\nIn considerazione del tempo da Lei dedicatoci, nelle prossime 6-8 settimane Le invieremo un compenso di $"+hono+" al seguente indirizzo:\n\n"+fulladdress+"\n\n Se desidera ricevere delucidazioni sullo studio o sul pagamento del Suo compenso, La invitiamo ad utilizzare il seguente NUMERO DI CONFERMA: "+confirmationnum+". Per ulteriori informazioni, ci contatti allindirizzo:\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nCordiali saluti.\n\nLaura Malett\nCoordinatrice della Ricerca\n";
		break;

		default:

		//Cheque
		if (f('BG_HonoType') == 1)
			hono = f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel() + " of " + f('BG_HonoAmount') + " " + f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel();
		else
			hono = "of " + f('BG_HonoAmount') + " " + f('BG_HonoCurr').valueLabel() + " in " + f('BG_HonoType').valueLabel();

		subj = servicename + " participation confirmation " + projnumber;
		
		msg = servicename + " thanks you for your successful participation in this study.";
		msg = msg + "\n\nIn appreciation of your time an honorarium " + hono;
		msg = msg + " will be sent to you in the next 6-8 weeks to this address:\n\n";
		msg = msg + fulladdress;
		msg = msg + "\n\nPlease use the following CONFIRMATION NUMBER if you have any questions about the ";
		msg = msg + "study or payment of your honorarium: " + confirmationnum;
		msg = msg + ". Should you have any queries, you can contact us at:";
		msg = msg + "\n\nlauram@pslresearch.com\n\nBest Regards,\nLaura Malett\nResearch Coordinator\n";
		} 

	//send mail:
	SendMail("lauram@pslresearch.com", emailAddress, subj, msg);
	
	//Verification that confirmation email has been sent
	f('mail_sent').set(1);
	}

<script>
// Set the return question (qReturn=q1) and the html folder and filename (/projectName/pnumber.html)
// You will have to create a seperate html file for each language
location = "http://hab.pslresearch.com/images/projectName/pnumber.html?r=^CurrentID()^&s=^CurrentSID()^&qReturn=q1";
</script>

</script>
